TEST17

  S(X) over a region (of any dimension), assuming:
 
  * that there is a set of finite element basis
    functions PSI;

    elements whose areas are known;
  * that the integral is to be computed by a quadrature
    rule applied in the same way to each element;
  * that the value of the basis functions is given
    at every quadrature node in every element;
